SQL> SELECT NCONST||','||primaryname||','||startyear||','||counter
  2  FROM (SELECT NB.NCONST,NB.primaryname,TB.startyear,COUNT(*) AS counter
  3  FROM imdb00.name_basics NB, imdb00.title_principals TP, imdb00.title_basics TB
  4  WHERE NB.nconst = TP.nconst AND 
  5          TP.tconst = TB.tconst AND 
  6          LOWER(TB.titleType) = 'movie' AND
  7          LOWER(TP.category) IN ('actor') AND TB.startyear NOT LIKE '\N' AND
  8          TB.startyear > '1961' AND
  9          TB.startyear < '1972'
 10  GROUP BY NB.nconst, NB.primaryname, TB.startyear
 11  ORDER BY TB.startyear)
 12  WHERE counter = (SELECT MAX(counter) 
 13  FROM (SELECT NB.primaryname,TB.startyear,COUNT(*) AS counter
 14  FROM imdb00.name_basics NB, imdb00.title_principals TP, imdb00.title_basics TB
 15  WHERE NB.nconst = TP.nconst AND 
 16          TP.tconst = TB.tconst AND 
 17          LOWER(TB.titleType) = 'movie' AND
 18          LOWER(TP.category) IN ('actor') AND TB.startyear NOT LIKE '\N' AND
 19          TB.startyear > '1961' AND
 20          TB.startyear < '1972'
 21  GROUP BY NB.nconst, NB.primaryname, TB.startyear
 22  ORDER BY TB.startyear));

SQL> SELECT NB.NCONST||'.'||NB.primaryname||','||TB.startyear||','||COUNT(*)
  2  FROM imdb00.name_basics NB, imdb00.title_principals TP, imdb00.title_basics TB
  3  WHERE NB.nconst = TP.nconst AND 
  4          TP.tconst = TB.tconst AND 
  5          LOWER(TB.titleType) = 'movie' AND
  6          LOWER(TP.category) IN ('actor') AND TB.startyear NOT LIKE '\N'
  7  GROUP BY NB.nconst, NB.primaryname, TB.startyear
  8  HAVING TB.startyear > '1961' AND
  9          TB.startyear < '1972' AND
 10          COUNT(*) = 3
 11  ORDER BY TB.startyear;

SQL> SELECT NB.NCONST||'.'||NB.primaryname||','||TB.startyear||','||COUNT(*)
  2  FROM imdb00.name_basics NB, imdb00.title_principals TP, imdb00.title_basics TB
  3  WHERE NB.nconst = TP.nconst AND 
  4          TP.tconst = TB.tconst AND 
  5          LOWER(TB.titleType) = 'movie' AND
  6          LOWER(TP.category) IN ('actress') AND TB.startyear NOT LIKE '\N'
  7  GROUP BY NB.nconst, NB.primaryname, TB.startyear
  8  HAVING TB.startyear > '1961' AND
  9          TB.startyear < '1972' AND
 10          COUNT(*) = 3
 11  ORDER BY TB.startyear;

SQL> --Query:MAX movies by an actor in years 1962-1971
SQL> --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SQL> SELECT NCONST||','||primaryname||','||startyear||','||counter
  2  FROM (SELECT NB.NCONST,NB.primaryname,TB.startyear,COUNT(*) AS counter
  3  FROM imdb00.name_basics NB, imdb00.title_principals TP, imdb00.title_basics TB
  4  WHERE NB.nconst = TP.nconst AND 
  5          TP.tconst = TB.tconst AND 
  6          LOWER(TB.titleType) = 'movie' AND
  7          LOWER(TP.category) IN ('actor') AND TB.startyear NOT LIKE '\N' AND
  8          TB.startyear > '1961' AND
  9          TB.startyear < '1972'
 10  GROUP BY NB.nconst, NB.primaryname, TB.startyear
 11  ORDER BY TB.startyear)
 12  WHERE counter = (SELECT MAX(counter) 
 13  FROM (SELECT NB.primaryname,TB.startyear,COUNT(*) AS counter
 14  FROM imdb00.name_basics NB, imdb00.title_principals TP, imdb00.title_basics TB
 15  WHERE NB.nconst = TP.nconst AND 
 16          TP.tconst = TB.tconst AND 
 17          LOWER(TB.titleType) = 'movie' AND
 18          LOWER(TP.category) IN ('actor') AND TB.startyear NOT LIKE '\N' AND
 19          TB.startyear > '1961' AND
 20          TB.startyear < '1972'
 21  GROUP BY NB.nconst, NB.primaryname, TB.startyear
 22  ORDER BY TB.startyear));

SQL> --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SQL> --Query:MIN 3 movies by an actor in years 1962-1971
SQL> --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SQL> SELECT NB.NCONST||'.'||NB.primaryname||','||TB.startyear||','||COUNT(*)
  2  FROM imdb00.name_basics NB, imdb00.title_principals TP, imdb00.title_basics TB
  3  WHERE NB.nconst = TP.nconst AND 
  4          TP.tconst = TB.tconst AND 
  5          LOWER(TB.titleType) = 'movie' AND
  6          LOWER(TP.category) IN ('actor') AND TB.startyear NOT LIKE '\N'
  7  GROUP BY NB.nconst, NB.primaryname, TB.startyear
  8  HAVING TB.startyear > '1961' AND
  9          TB.startyear < '1972' AND
 10          COUNT(*) = 3
 11  ORDER BY TB.startyear;

SQL> --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SQL> --Query:MIN 3 movies by an actress in years 1962-1971
SQL> --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SQL> SELECT NB.NCONST||'.'||NB.primaryname||','||TB.startyear||','||COUNT(*)
  2  FROM imdb00.name_basics NB, imdb00.title_principals TP, imdb00.title_basics TB
  3  WHERE NB.nconst = TP.nconst AND 
  4          TP.tconst = TB.tconst AND 
  5          LOWER(TB.titleType) = 'movie' AND
  6          LOWER(TP.category) IN ('actress') AND TB.startyear NOT LIKE '\N'
  7  GROUP BY NB.nconst, NB.primaryname, TB.startyear
  8  HAVING TB.startyear > '1961' AND
  9          TB.startyear < '1972' AND
 10          COUNT(*) = 3
 11  ORDER BY TB.startyear;
